<script type="text/javascript">
	function toggle(showHideDiv) {
		var ele = document.getElementById(showHideDiv);

		if(ele.style.display == "block") {
			ele.style.display = "none";
		} else {
			ele.style.display = "block";
		}
	}

	function ControlFunction(control_name) {
		var x = document.getElementsByClassName(control_name);
		var i;

		for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
			if (x[i].style.display == "block") {
				x[i].style.display = "none";
			} else {
				x[i].style.display = "block";
			}
		}
	}

	function Enrl_ControlFunction() {
		ControlFunction("Enr_Contr");
	}

	function Inf_ControlFunction() {
		ControlFunction("Inf_Cor");
	}
</script>

					<table class="tb_search">

										<b> Enrolment Control: A</b>
<br>
<b>SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES</b>
<br>
<b>Step 1:</b> 
Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below). 
<br>
<b>Step 2:</b>
Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at the Office of the Registrar (Highland Hall, First Floor). Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students should contact the office listed for more information.
<br>
<b>Step 3:</b>
Submit the signed Supervised Study form to HL238 one week prior to the last day to add courses for the session. Staff will ensure your course status on ACORN will be updated from interim (INT) to approved (APP). 
<br>
<b>Anthropology Office HL238</b>

<b>SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES</b>
<br>
<b>Step 1:</b> 
Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below). 
<br>
<b>Step 2:</b>
Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at the Registrar's Office (Highland Hall, First Floor). Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information.
<br>
<b>Step 3:</b>
Submit the signed Supervised Study form to the Registrar's Office by the last day to add courses for the session. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

										<b> Enrolment Control: P</b>
<br>
Initially, CSC courses are open to all UTSC CSC program students, and all other UTSC students who require this course for their program. Students must also meet the course pre-requisite(s). 
<br>
<br>
Starting shortly after <b>Friday, April 12th 3:00pm</b>, B-, C- and D-level CSC courses will be opened to all UTSC students who meet the pre-requisites. Students who do not require this course for their program must meet additional Cumulative GPA (CGPA) requirements: 
<br>
*A student who is not in a CSC program and does not have a CGPA of at least 3.0 may not take any B- level CSC course, with exception of CSCB20H3. 
<br>
*A student who is not in a CSC program and does not have a CGPA of at least 3.0 may not take any C- or D-level CSC course. 
<br>
*When a B-, C-, or D-level CSC course approaches its capacity, CSC program students will be given preference for further enrollment over non-CSC program students. 
<br>
<br>
Refer to the computer science section of the calendar for more information on admission to courses.

<b>Step 1:</b> Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
<br> 
<b>Step 2:</b> Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at the Office of the Registrar (Highland Hall, First Floor). Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information. 
<br>
<b>Step 3:</b> 
Submit the signed Supervised Study form to the Office of the Registrar by the last day to add courses for the session. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from (INT) to approved (APP).

										<b>Enrolment Control: P</b> 
<br>
<br>
<b>This is an intensive, 1.0 credit course offered across a six-week period combining FREA96H3 and FREA97H3. Students will be expected to attend class up to 12 hours per week. </b>
<br>
<br>
You may only enroll in this course if you have zero knowledge of French and no prior exposure to the language. 
<br>
<br>
Please note that your proficiency will be assessed by the course instructor during the first week of class and monitored throughout the term. If they feel that you were not truthful and honest regarding your proficiency in French, they reserve the right to have you removed from the course at any point in the semester on the grounds of academic dishonesty.
<br>
<br>
<b>Period 1</b>: Enrollment will be restricted to students in the Management and International Business (MIB) program, Specialist (Coop and non-coop) in Linguistics, Major (Coop and non-coop) in Linguistics, and Specialist (Coop) in International Development Studies (both arts and science streams). 
<br>
<br>
<b> Period 2 </b>: This course may open to students in other UTSC programs shortly after <b>3:00pm on Monday, April 15th</b>, space permitting.

<br>
<b>SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES</b>
<br>
<b>Step 1:</b> 
Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below). 
<br>
<b>Step 2:</b>
Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at Office of the Registrar (Highland Hall, First Floor). Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students should contact the office listed for more information.
<br>
<b>Step 3:</b>
Submit the signed Supervised Study form to HL234 one week prior to the last day to add courses for the session. Staff will ensure your course status on ACORN will be updated from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

Students should contact the Office listed for more information. 
<br>
<b>Step 3:</b> Submit the signed Supervised Study form to the Office of the Registrar by the last day to add courses for the session. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

										<b> Enrolment Control: RP</b>
<br>
<b>Students in Co-op Management Programs </b>
<br>
Until <b>4:00pm on Monday, April 1st</b> enrolment in Management courses (except MGTA01 and MGTA02) is restricted to co-op management students. 
<br>
Enrolment in B, C and D level Economics courses is restricted to Co-op Management, Economics and IDS students. Priority is necessary as these students must take specific Management courses in the Summer, in order to participate in the Fall/Winter work study terms. Students may add other courses as soon as their course enrolment start time begins. 
<br>
<br>
<b>Non Co-op Management and Economics students</b>
<br> 
Shortly after <b>4:00pm on Monday, April 1st</b> enrolment in Management courses (except MGTA01 and MGTA02) and B, C, and D level Economics courses will open up. Students may add other courses as soon as their course enrolment start time begins. 
<br>
<br>
Visiting students need to obtain permission from the Academic Director to enroll in Management courses.

Students may add other courses as soon as their course enrolment start time begins. 
<br>
<br>
<b>Non Co-op Management and Economics students</b>
<br>

<br>
<br>
Visiting students need to obtain permission from the Academic Director to enroll in Management courses.

If the course you need is full, please add yourself to the waitlist.
<br>
<br>
<b>Period 3:</b> Starting shortly after <b>4:00pm on Wednesday April 3rd</b>, all MGE courses with remaining space will be opened up to all UTSC students. Students not in the program, including Minors in Economics, <b>ARE REQUIRED</b> to have a CGPA of 2.0 or better if they want to enroll in in <b>MGEB02H3, MGEB06H3, MGEB11H3, MGEB12H3, MGEC02H3, MGEC06H3, and MGEC11H3</b>. <b>SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES</b>
<br> 
<b>Step 1:</b> Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below). 
<br>
<b>Step 2:</b> Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at the Office of the Registrar (Highland Hall, First Floor). Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information. 
<br>
<b>Step 3:</b> Submit the signed Supervised Study form to the Office of the Registrar by the last day to add courses for the session. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

Until <b>4:00pm on Monday, April 1st</b> enrolment in Management courses (except MGTA01 and MGTA02) is restricted to co-op management students. 
<br>
Enrolment in B, C and D level Economics courses is restricted to Co-op Management, Economics and IDS students. Priority is necessary as these students must take specific Management courses in the Summer, in order to participate in the Fall/Winter work study terms. Students may add other courses as soon as their course enrolment start time begins. 
<br>
<br>
<b>Non Co-op Management and Economics students</b>
<br> 
Shortly after <b>4:00pm on Monday, April 1st</b> enrolment in Management courses (except MGTA01 and MGTA02) and B, C, and D level Economics courses will open up. Students may add other courses as soon as their course enrolment start time begins. 
<br>
<br>
Visiting students need to obtain permission from the Academic Director to enroll in Management courses.
